<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окаменеть.html>окамене́ть</a> (8943)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каменеть.html>камене́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kamenétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окаменеть.html>окамене́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okamenétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каменеть.html>камене́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">окаменева́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn to stone, to petrify</li>
<li><i>(with fear, shock etc)</i> to petrify, to be petrified</li>
<li>to harden, to become embittered</li></ol>

<p>Has the form of a past passive participle of the dated verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ока́ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but with shifted stress.

***окидывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окидывать.html>оки́дывать</a> (26127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">окид-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okid-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окидывать.html>оки́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okídyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окинуть.html>оки́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to scan (with one's eyes)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:окидывать.html>оки́дывать</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгля́дом</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okídyvatʹ</b> štó-libo vzgljádom</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to scan something, to cast one's eyes over something</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***окинуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окинуть.html>оки́нуть</a> (9238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окинуть.html>оки́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окидывать.html>оки́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to scan (with one's eyes)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:окинуть.html>оки́нуть</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:взгляд.html>взгля́дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>okínutʹ</b> štó-libo vzgljádom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scan something, to cast one's eyes over something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кидать.html>кида́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kidátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кидаться.html>кида́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kidátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуться.html>ки́нуться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kínutʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***оккупация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оккупация.html>оккупа́ция</a> (9383)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">occupātio</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оккупация.html>оккупа́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okkupácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оккупация.html>оккупа́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оккупация.html>оккупа́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оккупация.html>оккупа́ций</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оккупировать.html>оккупи́ровать</a> (9138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">okkupieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оклеветать.html>оклевета́ть</a> (22122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеветать.html>клевета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klevetátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оклеветать.html>оклевета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oklevetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to slander, to defame, to malign</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеветать.html>клевета́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">klevetátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наклевета́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">naklevetátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***оклеить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оклеить.html>окле́ить</a> (20404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеить.html>кле́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kléitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оклеить.html>окле́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">okléitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">окле́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover by glueing (e.g. a wall with wallpaper)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">окле́ивание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">okléivanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">окле́йка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">okléjka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оклематься.html>оклема́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oklemátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окликать.html>оклика́ть</a> (16442)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окликнуть.html>окли́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oklíknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***окно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно</a> (217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*okъno</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oknó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>о́кна</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>о́кон</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>window
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">smotrétʹ v <b>oknó</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to look through a <b>window</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***око.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>око</a> (4603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oko</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃ekʷ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́ко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óko</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:око.html>о́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́чи</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:око.html>оче́й</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* <i><b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́чи</a></span></b></i> is actually an old nominative dual form for neuter nouns.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or poetic or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> eye (used in proverbs and expressions)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́чи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрные</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>óči</b> čórnyje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dark eyes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́ко</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зу́б</a> неймёт.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vídit <b>óko</b>, da zúb nejmjót.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>The eye</b> sees (it) but the tooth cannot take it.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
